(function(){

  /* ════ NOTE PICKER ════ */
  const CW_NOTES_FR={nat:['Do','Ré','Mi','Fa','Sol','La','Si'],sha:['Do#','Ré#',null,'Fa#','Sol#','La#',null],fla:['Réb','Mib',null,'Solb','Lab','Sib',null]};
  const CW_OCTAVES=['2','3','4','5','6'];
  var cwPickerInput=null,cwPickerNote='',cwPickerOctave='';

  function initCwPicker(){
    var N=CW_NOTES_FR;
    $('cw-np-naturals').innerHTML=N.nat.map(function(n){return '<button class="cw-np-btn" onclick="cwPickerSetNote(''+n+'')">'+n+'</button>';}).join('');
    $('cw-np-sharps').innerHTML=N.sha.map(function(n){return n?'<button class="cw-np-btn cw-sha" onclick="cwPickerSetNote(''+n+'')">'+n+'</button>':'<span style="min-width:33px;display:inline-block"></span>';}).join('');
    $('cw-np-flats').innerHTML=N.fla.map(function(n){return n?'<button class="cw-np-btn cw-fla" onclick="cwPickerSetNote(''+n+'')">'+n+'</button>':'<span style="min-width:33px;display:inline-block"></span>';}).join('');
    $('cw-np-octaves').innerHTML=CW_OCTAVES.map(function(o){return '<button class="cw-np-oct-btn" onclick="cwPickerSetOctave(''+o+'')">'+o+'</button>';}).join('');
  }
  function cwShowPicker(input){
    cwPickerInput=input;cwPickerNote='';cwPickerOctave='';
    var v=input.value.trim();
    if(v){var m=v.match(/^(.+?)([2-6])$/);if(m){cwPickerNote=m[1];cwPickerOctave=m[2];}else cwPickerNote=v;}
    cwUpdatePickerHL();cwUpdatePickerPreview();
    var pk=$('cw-note-picker');pk.classList.remove('cw-hidden');
    var rect=input.getBoundingClientRect();
    var pw=pk.offsetWidth||305,ph=pk.offsetHeight||280;
    var top=rect.bottom+window.scrollY+6,left=rect.left+window.scrollX;
    if(left+pw>window.innerWidth-10)left=window.innerWidth-pw-10;
    if(left<8)left=8;
    if(top+ph>window.scrollY+window.innerHeight-10)top=rect.top+window.scrollY-ph-6;
    pk.style.top=Math.max(8,top)+'px';pk.style.left=Math.max(8,left)+'px';
    input.classList.add('cw-picker-open');
  }
  function cwHidePicker(){
    $('cw-note-picker').classList.add('cw-hidden');
    if(cwPickerInput){cwPickerInput.classList.remove('cw-picker-open');cwPickerInput=null;}
    cwPickerNote='';cwPickerOctave='';
  }
  function cwPickerSetNote(n){cwPickerNote=n;cwUpdatePickerHL();cwUpdatePickerPreview();if(cwPickerNote&&cwPickerOctave)cwPickerInsert();}
  function cwPickerSetOctave(o){cwPickerOctave=o;cwUpdatePickerHL();cwUpdatePickerPreview();if(cwPickerNote&&cwPickerOctave)cwPickerInsert();}
  function cwPickerInsert(){
    if(!cwPickerInput)return;
    var v=cwPickerNote+cwPickerOctave;if(!v)return;
    cwPickerInput.value=v;
    cwPickerInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('input',{bubbles:true}));
    cwPickerInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('change',{bubbles:true}));
    cwHidePicker();
  }
  function cwPickerClear(){
    if(!cwPickerInput)return;
    cwPickerInput.value='';
    cwPickerInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('input',{bubbles:true}));
    cwPickerInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('change',{bubbles:true}));
    cwPickerNote='';cwPickerOctave='';cwUpdatePickerHL();cwUpdatePickerPreview();cwHidePicker();
  }
  function cwUpdatePickerHL(){
    widget.querySelectorAll('#cw-np-naturals .cw-np-btn,#cw-np-sharps .cw-np-btn,#cw-np-flats .cw-np-btn').forEach(function(b){b.classList.toggle('cw-sel',b.textContent===cwPickerNote);});
    widget.querySelectorAll('#cw-np-octaves .cw-np-oct-btn').forEach(function(b){b.classList.toggle('cw-sel',b.textContent===cwPickerOctave);});
  }
  function cwUpdatePickerPreview(){
    $('cw-np-preview-text').textContent=(cwPickerNote+cwPickerOctave)||'— sélectionnez note + octave —';
  }

(intérieure)","nb":10}],"notes":{"droite":[[{"p":"Sol#3","t":"Si3"},{"p":"La3","t":"Ré4"},{"p":"Mib4","t":"Sol4"},{"p":"Sol#4","t":"Si4"},{"p":"La4","t":"Ré5"},{"p":"Mib5","t":"Sol5"},{"p":"Sol#5","t":"Si5"},{"p":"La5","t":"Ré6"},{"p":"Mib6","t":"Sol6"},{"p":"Sol#6","t":"Si6"},{"p":"La6","t":"Ré7"}],[{"p":"Mi3","t":"Sol#3"},{"p":"Fa#3","t":"Sib3"},{"p":"La3","t":"Do#4"},{"p":"Do4","t":"Sol4"},{"p":"Mi4","t":"Sol#4"},{"p":"Fa#4","t":"Sib4"},{"p":"La4","t":"Do#5"},{"p":"Do5","t":"Sol5"},{"p":"Mi5","t":"Sol#5"},{"p":"Fa#5","t":"Sib5"},{"p":"La5","t":"Do#6"}],[{"p":"Sol3","t":"La3"},{"p":"Do4","t":"Si3"},{"p":"Mi4","t":"Ré4"},{"p":"Sol4","t":"Fa#4"},{"p":"Do5","t":"La4"},{"p":"Mi5","t":"Do5"},{"p":"Sol5","t":"Ré5"},{"p":"Do6","t":"Mi5"},{"p":"Mi6","t":"La5"},{"p":"Sol6","t":"Do6"}]],"basses":[{"p":"Sol2","t":"Ré2"},{"p":"Do3","t":"Sol2"},{"p":"Ré3","t":"La2"},{"p":"La3","t":"Mi3"}],"accords":[{"p":"Sol2","t":"Ré2"},{"p":"Do3","t":"Sol2"},{"p":"Ré3","t":"La2"},{"p":"La3","t":"Mi3"}],"terzetto":[],"basses2":[{"p":"Sol2","t":"Ré2"},{"p":"Do3","t":"Sol2"},{"p":"Ré3","t":"La2"},{"p":"La3","t":"Mi3"}],"basses3":[{"p":"Sol2","t":"Ré2"},{"p":"Do3","t":"Sol2"},{"p":"Ré3","t":"La2"},{"p":"La3","t":"Mi3"}],"accords2":[{"p":"Ré3","t":"La2"},{"p":"Sol3","t":"Ré3"},{"p":"La3","t":"Mi3"},{"p":"Mi4","t":"Si3"}],"accords3":[{"p":"","t":""},{"p":"","t":""},{"p":"","t":""},{"p":"","t":""}]}}};

  /* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
     STATE
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  let currentPreset = null;   // raw preset JSON
  let currentData = null;     // data object for SVG rendering
  let darkMode = false;
  const LS_KEY = 'clavier-widget-plans';

  /* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
     DOM HELPERS
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  const $ = function(id){ return document.getElementById(id); };
  const widget = document.querySelector('.clavier-widget');

  /* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
     SVG HELPERS (from the main tool)
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  let _svgId = 0;
  function svg_open(w, h, bg){
    var id = 'cwvp' + (++_svgId);
    return '<svg width="'+w+'" height="'+h+'" viewBox="0 0 '+w+' '+h+'" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" font-family="system-ui,\'Segoe UI\',Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif" overflow="hidden"><defs><clipPath id="'+id+'"><rect width="'+w+'" height="'+h+'"/></clipPath></defs><rect width="'+w+'" height="'+h+'" fill="'+(bg||'white')+'"/><g clip-path="url(#'+id+')">';
  }
  function svg_close(){ return '</g></svg>'; }
  function tx(x, y, text, size, fill, weight, anchor){
    return '<text x="'+x+'" y="'+y+'" font-size="'+size+'" fill="'+fill+'" font-weight="'+(weight||'normal')+'" text-anchor="'+(anchor||'start')+'">'+text+'</text>';
  }
  function escSVG(s){
    if(!s) return '';
    return String(s).replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;');
  }
  function fmtDate(d){
    if(!d) return new Date().toLocaleDateString('fr-FR');
    try{ return new Date(d).toLocaleDateString('fr-FR'); }catch(e){ return d; }
  }
  function displayNote(n){ return n || ''; }
  function dn(note){ return escSVG(displayNote(note)); }

  function svgBtnVal(v, cx, baseY, color){
    if(!v) return '';
    var disp = displayNote(v);
    if(!disp.includes('/')){
      var fs = disp.length > 8 ? 5.5 : disp.length > 5 ? 6.8 : 8;
      return tx(cx, baseY, escSVG(disp), fs, color, 'bold', 'middle');
    }
    var parts = disp.split('/').map(function(p){ return p.trim(); }).filter(Boolean);
    var lineH = 6.5, fs2 = 5.5;
    var startY = baseY - ((parts.length - 1) * lineH) / 2;
    var out = '<text font-size="'+fs2+'" fill="'+color+'" font-weight="bold" text-anchor="middle">';
    parts.forEach(function(p, i){ out += '<tspan x="'+cx+'" y="'+(startY + i * lineH)+'">'+escSVG(p)+'</tspan>'; });
    return out + '</text>';
  }

  /* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
     buildSVG_Plan (from lines 2048-2366, t() replaced)
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  function buildSVG_Plan(data, dark){
    var R = 18;
    var BGAP = 46;
    var CGAP = 52;
    var MH = 20, MT = 14, MB = 30;
    var TITLE_H = 76;
    var BTWN = 50;

    var gold2  = dark ? '#c9a227' : '#4338CA';
    var bg     = dark ? '#111' : '#fff';
    var pushBg = dark ? '#0d1f0d' : '#EEF2FF';
    var pullBg = dark ? '#1f1000' : '#FFFBEB';
    var pushTx = dark ? '#6fcf5a' : '#3730A3';
    var pullTx = dark ? '#e8b840' : '#92400E';
    var pushTx2= dark ? 'rgba(111,207,90,.55)' : 'rgba(55,48,163,.5)';
    var pullTx2= dark ? 'rgba(232,184,64,.55)' : 'rgba(146,64,14,.5)';
    var subtl  = dark ? '#888866' : '#94A3B8';
    var stroke = dark ? '#c9a227' : '#6366F1';
    var numTx  = dark ? 'rgba(200,162,39,.3)' : 'rgba(99,102,241,.2)';
    var band1  = dark ? '#1a1a1a' : '#FAFAFA';
    var band2  = dark ? '#161616' : '#F5F3FF';
    var circleBorder = dark ? '#333' : '#C7D2FE';
    var textColor    = dark ? '#ccc' : '#1E293B';
    var ruleColor    = dark ? '#444' : '#E2E8F0';

    function drawBtn(cx, cy, btn, btn2, editId){
      var o = '';
      if(editId) o += '<g class="cw-edit-btn" data-edit="'+editId+'">'
      o += '<circle cx="'+cx+'" cy="'+cy+'" r="'+R+'" fill="'+bg+'" stroke="'+circleBorder+'" stroke-width="1"/>';
      o += '<path d="M'+(cx-R)+','+cy+' A'+R+','+R+' 0 0,1 '+(cx+R)+','+cy+'" fill="'+pushBg+'"/>';
      o += '<path d="M'+(cx-R)+','+cy+' A'+R+','+R+' 0 0,0 '+(cx+R)+','+cy+'" fill="'+pullBg+'"/>';
      o += '<circle cx="'+cx+'" cy="'+cy+'" r="'+R+'" fill="none" stroke="'+stroke+'" stroke-width="1.2"/>';
      o += '<line x1="'+(cx-R)+'" y1="'+cy+'" x2="'+(cx+R)+'" y2="'+cy+'" stroke="'+stroke+'" stroke-width=".5" opacity=".4"/>';
      var b2ok = btn2 && (btn2.p || btn2.t);
      if(b2ok){
        if(btn.p)  o += svgBtnVal(btn.p, cx, cy-11, pushTx);
        if(btn2.p) o += svgBtnVal(btn2.p, cx, cy-4, pushTx2);
        if(btn.t)  o += svgBtnVal(btn.t, cx, cy+8, pullTx);
        if(btn2.t) o += svgBtnVal(btn2.t, cx, cy+15, pullTx2);
      } else {
        if(btn.p) o += svgBtnVal(btn.p, cx, cy-7, pushTx);
        if(btn.t) o += svgBtnVal(btn.t, cx, cy+15, pullTx);
      }
      if(editId) o += '</g>';
      return o;
    }

    var rhRows = data.droite;
    var nRH = rhRows.length;
    var maxRHBtns = Math.max.apply(null, rhRows.map(function(r){ return r.boutons.length; }).concat([1]));

    var isPaired = data.lhDisplayMode === 'paired';
    var lhSecRows = [];

    if(isPaired){
      var nPairs = Math.max(data.basses.length, data.accords.length);
      var ppRow  = Math.max(1, data.lhPairsPerRow || nPairs);
      var vA = data.nbVoixAccords || 2, vB = data.nbVoixBasses || 2;
      if(data.lhPairedDir === 'horizontal'){
        var nGroups = Math.ceil(nPairs / ppRow);
        for(var c = 0; c < ppRow; c++){
          var intItems=[], intItems2=[], intTypes=[], intIndices=[];
          for(var g = 0; g < nGroups; g++){
            var ii = g * ppRow + c;
            if(ii >= nPairs) break;
            var seq = data.lhBassFirst
              ? [['B',data.basses,data.basses2,vB],['A',data.accords,data.accords2,vA]]
              : [['A',data.accords,data.accords2,vA],['B',data.basses,data.basses2,vB]];
            seq.forEach(function(x){
              var typ=x[0],src=x[1],src2=x[2],nv=x[3];
              if(src[ii]){ intItems.push(src[ii]); intItems2.push(nv>1&&src2?src2[ii]||null:null); intTypes.push(typ); intIndices.push(ii+1); }
            });
          }
          if(intItems.length){
            var lbl = ppRow===1 ? 'Basses / Accords' : 'Basses/Accords '+(c+1);
            lhSecRows.push({nom:lbl,items:intItems,items2:intItems2,offset:0,interleavedTypes:intTypes,interleavedIndices:intIndices});
          }
        }
      } else {
        var nGroups2 = Math.ceil(nPairs / ppRow);
        for(var g2 = 0; g2 < nGroups2; g2++){
          var s0 = g2*ppRow, s1 = Math.min(s0+ppRow, nPairs);
          var intItems3=[], intItems4=[], intTypes2=[], intIndices2=[];
          for(var i2 = s0; i2 < s1; i2++){
            var seq2 = data.lhBassFirst
              ? [['B',data.basses,data.basses2,vB],['A',data.accords,data.accords2,vA]]
              : [['A',data.accords,data.accords2,vA],['B',data.basses,data.basses2,vB]];
            seq2.forEach(function(x){
              var typ=x[0],src=x[1],src2=x[2],nv=x[3];
              if(src[i2]){ intItems3.push(src[i2]); intItems4.push(nv>1&&src2?src2[i2]||null:null); intTypes2.push(typ); intIndices2.push(i2+1); }
            });
          }
          var lbl2 = nGroups2===1 ? 'Basses / Accords' : 'Basses/Accords '+(g2+1);
          lhSecRows.push({nom:lbl2,items:intItems3,items2:intItems4,offset:0,interleavedTypes:intTypes2,interleavedIndices:intIndices2});
        }
      }
      if(data.terzetto && data.terzetto.length) lhSecRows.push({nom:'Terzetto',items:data.terzetto,items2:null,offset:0,src:'terzetto',startIdx:0});
    } else {
      var lhRowCfg = (data.lhRows && data.lhRows.length) ? data.lhRows : [{nb:data.basses.length||1,offset:0}];
      var accSecs=[], basSecs=[];
      var bIdx=0, aIdx=0;
      var vA2 = data.nbVoixAccords||2, vB2 = data.nbVoixBasses||2;
      lhRowCfg.forEach(function(row, ri){
        accSecs.push({nom:lhRowCfg.length===1?'Accords':(ri===0?'Accords':'\u21b3+'+aIdx),items:data.accords.slice(aIdx,aIdx+row.nb),items2:vA2>1?(data.accords2||[]).slice(aIdx,aIdx+row.nb):null,offset:row.offset||0,src:'accords',startIdx:aIdx});
        aIdx += row.nb;
        basSecs.push({nom:lhRowCfg.length===1?'Basses':(ri===0?'Basses':'\u21b3+'+bIdx),items:data.basses.slice(bIdx,bIdx+row.nb),items2:vB2>1?(data.basses2||[]).slice(bIdx,bIdx+row.nb):null,offset:row.offset||0,src:'basses',startIdx:bIdx});
        bIdx += row.nb;
      });
      if(data.lhBassFirst){ basSecs.forEach(function(s2){lhSecRows.push(s2);}); accSecs.forEach(function(s2){lhSecRows.push(s2);}); }
      else                { accSecs.forEach(function(s2){lhSecRows.push(s2);}); basSecs.forEach(function(s2){lhSecRows.push(s2);}); }
      if(data.terzetto && data.terzetto.length) lhSecRows.push({nom:'Terzetto',items:data.terzetto,items2:null,offset:0,src:'terzetto',startIdx:0});
    }

    var nLH = lhSecRows.length;
    var maxLHBtns = nLH > 0 ? Math.max.apply(null, lhSecRows.map(function(sc){ return sc.items.length; }).concat([0])) : 0;
    var maxBtns = Math.max(maxRHBtns, maxLHBtns, 1);

    var rhOffsets = rhRows.map(function(r){ return r.offset||0; });
    var rhMaxOff = Math.max.apply(null, rhOffsets.concat([0]));
    var rhMinOff = Math.min.apply(null, rhOffsets.concat([0]));
    var rhTopShift = -rhMinOff * (BGAP/2);
    var rhBottomExtra = rhMaxOff * (BGAP/2);
    var lhOffsets = lhSecRows.map(function(s2){ return s2.offset||0; });
    var lhMaxOff = lhOffsets.length ? Math.max.apply(null, lhOffsets.concat([0])) : 0;
    var lhMinOff = lhOffsets.length ? Math.min.apply(null, lhOffsets.concat([0])) : 0;
    var lhTopShift = -lhMinOff * (BGAP/2);
    var lhBottomExtra = lhMaxOff * (BGAP/2);
    var HEADER_GAP = 120;

    var lhW = nLH > 0 ? nLH * CGAP : 0;
    var rhW = nRH * CGAP;
    var contentW = lhW + (nLH > 0 ? BTWN : 0) + rhW;
    var W = Math.max(contentW + 2*MH, 460);
    var extraOff = Math.max(rhTopShift + rhBottomExtra, lhTopShift + lhBottomExtra);
    var bodyH = maxBtns * BGAP + extraOff + HEADER_GAP + 20;
    var H = MT + TITLE_H + bodyH + MB;

    var contentTop = MT + TITLE_H;
    var contentBot = H - MB;
    var gridCenterY = contentTop + (contentBot - contentTop) * 0.55;
    var gridTop = Math.round(gridCenterY - bodyH/2) + HEADER_GAP;

    var rhX0 = MH + CGAP/2;
    var lhX0 = nLH > 0 ? rhX0 + rhW + BTWN : rhX0 + rhW;
    var sepX = nLH > 0 ? (rhX0 + (nRH-1)*CGAP + R + (lhX0 - R)) / 2 : rhX0 + rhW + BTWN/2;

    var s = svg_open(W, H, bg);

    // Accent bar at top
    s += '<rect x="0" y="0" width="'+W+'" height="3" fill="'+gold2+'"/>';

    // Title table
    var tblX = MH, tblY = MT;
    var rotW = 22;
    var tblInfoX = tblX + rotW + 6;
    var rowH = 16;
    var tblRows = 4;
    var tblH = tblRows * rowH;

    s += '<rect x="'+tblX+'" y="'+tblY+'" width="'+rotW+'" height="'+tblH+'" fill="'+gold2+'" opacity=".08" rx="3"/>';
    s += '<rect x="'+tblX+'" y="'+tblY+'" width="'+(rotW+244)+'" height="'+tblH+'" fill="none" stroke="'+ruleColor+'" stroke-width="1" rx="3"/>';
    s += '<line x1="'+(tblX+rotW)+'" y1="'+tblY+'" x2="'+(tblX+rotW)+'" y2="'+(tblY+tblH)+'" stroke="'+ruleColor+'" stroke-width="1"/>';
    for(var i3 = 1; i3 < tblRows; i3++)
      s += '<line x1="'+(tblX+rotW)+'" y1="'+(tblY+i3*rowH)+'" x2="'+(tblX+rotW+244)+'" y2="'+(tblY+i3*rowH)+'" stroke="'+ruleColor+'" stroke-width=".5"/>';

    var rotCx = tblX + rotW/2, rotCy = tblY + tblH/2;
    s += '<text x="'+rotCx+'" y="'+rotCy+'" text-anchor="middle" font-size="13" fill="'+gold2+'" font-weight="bold" transform="rotate(-90,'+rotCx+','+rotCy+')">'+escSVG('Plan de clavier')+'</text>';

    s += '<text x="'+tblInfoX+'" y="'+(tblY+rowH/2+4)+'" font-size="12" fill="'+gold2+'" font-weight="bold">'+escSVG(data.nomInstrument||'Accordéon Diatonique')+'</text>';
    var r2 = data.nomJoueur ? 'Client : '+data.nomJoueur : '';
    s += '<text x="'+tblInfoX+'" y="'+(tblY+rowH+rowH/2+3)+'" font-size="8.5" fill="'+textColor+'">'+escSVG(r2)+'</text>';
    var nBtnsRH = data.droite.reduce(function(a,r){ return a + r.boutons.length; }, 0);
    var nBasses = data.basses ? data.basses.length : 0;
    var nAccords = data.accords ? data.accords.length : 0;
    var r3 = nRH+' '+(nRH>1?'rangées':'rangée')+' ('+nBtnsRH+' boutons) \u00b7 '+nBasses+' basses \u00b7 '+nAccords+' accords';
    s += '<text x="'+tblInfoX+'" y="'+(tblY+2*rowH+rowH/2+3)+'" font-size="8" fill="'+textColor+'">'+escSVG(r3)+'</text>';
    s += '<text x="'+tblInfoX+'" y="'+(tblY+3*rowH+rowH/2+3)+'" font-size="7.5" fill="'+subtl+'">'+escSVG(data.nomLuthier)+'  \u00b7  '+escSVG(fmtDate(data.date))+'</text>';

    s += '<text x="'+(rhX0-R-6)+'" y="'+(gridTop-HEADER_GAP+4)+'" font-size="8.5" fill="'+subtl+'" font-style="italic">Haut (graves)</text>';

    // Push/pull legend
    var legR = 7, legX = W - MH - legR - 2, legY = tblY + tblH/2;
    s += '<circle cx="'+legX+'" cy="'+legY+'" r="'+legR+'" fill="'+bg+'" stroke="'+stroke+'" stroke-width="1"/>';
    s += '<path d="M'+(legX-legR)+','+legY+' A'+legR+','+legR+' 0 0,1 '+(legX+legR)+','+legY+'" fill="'+pushBg+'"/>';
    s += '<path d="M'+(legX-legR)+','+legY+' A'+legR+','+legR+' 0 0,0 '+(legX+legR)+','+legY+'" fill="'+pullBg+'"/>';
    s += '<circle cx="'+legX+'" cy="'+legY+'" r="'+legR+'" fill="none" stroke="'+stroke+'" stroke-width="1"/>';
    s += '<line x1="'+(legX-legR)+'" y1="'+legY+'" x2="'+(legX+legR)+'" y2="'+legY+'" stroke="'+stroke+'" stroke-width=".4" opacity=".4"/>';
    s += tx(legX-legR-3, legY-1, 'Poussé', 6, textColor, 'normal', 'end');
    s += tx(legX-legR-3, legY+7, 'Tiré', 6, textColor, 'normal', 'end');

    // RH columns
    s += tx(rhX0 + ((nRH-1)*CGAP)/2, gridTop-HEADER_GAP+6, 'Main Droite', 8.5, gold2, 'bold', 'middle');
    rhRows.forEach(function(row, ri){
      var cx = rhX0 + ri * CGAP;
      var off = rhTopShift + (row.offset||0) * (BGAP/2);
      var lblY = gridTop - 8;
      s += '<text x="'+cx+'" y="'+lblY+'" text-anchor="start" font-size="6.5" fill="'+gold2+'" font-weight="bold" transform="rotate(-90,'+cx+','+lblY+')">'+escSVG(row.nom)+'</text>';
      if(row.boutons.length){
        var cy0 = gridTop + off + BGAP/2;
        var bandY = cy0 - R - 3;
        var bandH = (row.boutons.length-1)*BGAP + 2*(R+3);
        s += '<rect x="'+(cx-R-3)+'" y="'+bandY+'" width="'+((R+3)*2)+'" height="'+bandH+'" rx="3" fill="'+(ri%2===0?band1:band2)+'" opacity=".6"/>';
      }
      var suffix = ri===0 ? '' : ri===1 ? "'" : "''";
      row.boutons.forEach(function(btn, bi){
        var cy = gridTop + off + bi*BGAP + BGAP/2;
        s += drawBtn(cx, cy, btn, null, 'rh:'+ri+':'+bi);
        s += tx(cx-R-1, cy+R+2, (bi+1)+suffix, 5.5, numTx, 'bold', 'start');
      });
    });

    // Bellows separator
    if(nLH > 0){
      var sepY1 = gridTop-2, sepY2 = gridTop + maxBtns*BGAP + extraOff + 2;
      s += '<line x1="'+sepX+'" y1="'+sepY1+'" x2="'+sepX+'" y2="'+sepY2+'" stroke="'+(dark?'#444':'#C7D2FE')+'" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-dasharray="6,4"/>';
      var sepMidY = (sepY1 + sepY2) / 2;
      s += '<text x="'+sepX+'" y="'+sepMidY+'" text-anchor="middle" font-size="6.5" fill="'+subtl+'" font-weight="bold" transform="rotate(-90,'+sepX+','+sepMidY+')">'+escSVG('— SOUFFLET —')+'</text>';
    }

    // LH columns
    if(nLH > 0 && maxLHBtns > 0){
      var rhBlockH = maxRHBtns * BGAP + rhTopShift + rhBottomExtra;
      var lhBlockH = maxLHBtns * BGAP + lhTopShift + lhBottomExtra;
      var lhGridTop = gridTop + Math.round((rhBlockH - lhBlockH)/2);

      s += tx(lhX0 + ((nLH-1)*CGAP)/2, lhGridTop - HEADER_GAP + 6, 'Main Gauche', 8.5, gold2, 'bold', 'middle');

      var bassLbl = dark ? '#5aa0d0' : '#1D4ED8';
      var accLbl  = dark ? '#d09040' : '#B45309';
      lhSecRows.forEach(function(sec, si){
        var cx = lhX0 + si * CGAP;
        var off = lhTopShift + (sec.offset||0) * (BGAP/2);
        var has2 = sec.items2 && sec.items2.some(function(x){ return x != null; });
        if(sec.items.length){
          var cy0 = lhGridTop + off + BGAP/2;
          var bandY = cy0 - R - 3;
          var bandH = (sec.items.length-1)*BGAP + 2*(R+3);
          s += '<rect x="'+(cx-R-3)+'" y="'+bandY+'" width="'+((R+3)*2)+'" height="'+bandH+'" rx="3" fill="'+(si%2===0?band1:band2)+'" opacity=".6"/>';
        }
        sec.items.forEach(function(btn, bi){
          var cy = lhGridTop + off + bi*BGAP + BGAP/2;
          var lhEditId = null;
          if(sec.interleavedTypes){
            var eTyp = sec.interleavedTypes[bi] === 'B' ? 'basses' : 'accords';
            var eIdx = sec.interleavedIndices ? (sec.interleavedIndices[bi] - 1) : bi;
            lhEditId = eTyp + ':' + eIdx;
          } else if(sec.src){
            lhEditId = sec.src + ':' + (sec.startIdx + bi);
          }
          s += drawBtn(cx, cy, btn, has2 ? (sec.items2[bi]||null) : null, lhEditId);
          if(sec.interleavedTypes){
            var typ = sec.interleavedTypes[bi];
            var idx = sec.interleavedIndices ? sec.interleavedIndices[bi] : '';
            s += tx(cx-R+4, cy-R-2, typ+idx, 5.5, typ==='B'?bassLbl:accLbl, 'bold', 'start');
          }
        });
      });
      var lhLastCx = lhX0 + (nLH-1)*CGAP;
      for(var i4 = 0; i4 < maxLHBtns; i4++)
        s += tx(lhLastCx+R+5, lhGridTop+i4*BGAP+BGAP/2+3, i4+1, 6, numTx, 'normal', 'start');
    }

    s += '<text x="'+(W/2)+'" y="'+(H-MB+12)+'" font-size="8.5" fill="'+textColor+'" font-style="italic" text-anchor="middle">\u2191 Aigus</text>';
    s += '<line x1="'+MH+'" y1="'+(H-MB+20)+'" x2="'+(W-MH)+'" y2="'+(H-MB+20)+'" stroke="'+ruleColor+'" stroke-width="1"/>';
    s += tx(MH, H-MB+28, escSVG(data.nomLuthier)+' \u2014 ewendaviau.com', 7, subtl, 'normal', 'start');

    s += svg_close();
    return s;
  }

  /* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
     toData — convert preset JSON to rendering format
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  function toData(rec){
    var nRec = rec.notes || {};
    var droiteNotes = nRec.droite || [];
    var droite = (rec.rangees || []).map(function(row, ri){
      return {
        nom: row.nom || ('Rangée '+(ri+1)),
        register: row.register || 'N',
        offset: row.offset || 0,
        boutons: droiteNotes[ri] || []
      };
    });
    return {
      nomInstrument: rec.nom || rec.label || '',
      nomJoueur: rec.joueur || '',
      nomLuthier: rec.luthier || "Ewen d'Aviau",
      date: rec.dateCreation || '',
      nbVoix: rec.nbVoix || 2,
      voixPerRow: rec.voixPerRow || [],
      nbVoixAccords: rec.nbVoixAccords || 2,
      nbVoixBasses: rec.nbVoixBasses || 2,
      lhDisplayMode: rec.lhDisplayMode || 'separated',
      lhPairedDir: rec.lhPairedDir || 'vertical',
      lhRows: rec.lhRows || [{nb: (nRec.basses||[]).length || 1, offset: 0}],
      lhPairsPerRow: rec.lhPairsPerRow || 2,
      lhBassFirst: rec.lhBassFirst || false,
      showMidi: false,
      droite: droite,
      basses: nRec.basses || [],
      basses2: nRec.basses2 || [],
      basses3: nRec.basses3 || [],
      accords: nRec.accords || [],
      accords2: nRec.accords2 || [],
      accords3: nRec.accords3 || [],
      terzetto: nRec.terzetto || [],
      orderSpecs: rec.orderSpecs || {}
    };
  }

  /* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
     POPULATE PRESET SELECTOR (grouped by category)
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  function populatePresetSelector(){
    var sel = $('cw-preset-sel');
    var cats = {};
    PRESET_CATALOG.forEach(function(p){
      if(!cats[p.category]) cats[p.category] = [];
      cats[p.category].push(p);
    });
    Object.keys(cats).forEach(function(cat){
      var og = document.createElement('optgroup');
      og.label = cat;
      cats[cat].forEach(function(p){
        var opt = document.createElement('option');
        opt.value = p.id;
        opt.textContent = p.label;
        og.appendChild(opt);
      });
      sel.appendChild(og);
    });
  }

  /* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
     FETCH PRESET & RENDER
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  function loadPreset(id){
    if(!id){ currentPreset = null; currentData = null; renderAll(); return; }
    var raw = PRESETS_DATA[id];
    if(!raw){ $('cw-svg-wrap').innerHTML = '<p style="color:#c0392b;padding:12px;">Preset introuvable : ' + id + '</p>'; return; }
    var json = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(raw)); // deep clone
    var cat = PRESET_CATALOG.find(function(p){ return p.id === id; });
    if(cat) json.label = cat.label;
    currentPreset = json;
    applyUIToPreset();
    renderAll();
  }

  /* Apply UI field overrides to preset */
  function applyUIToPreset(){
    if(!currentPreset) return;
    var nom = $('cw-nom-instrument').value.trim();
    if(nom) currentPreset.nom = nom;
    var joueur = $('cw-nom-joueur').value.trim();
    currentPreset.joueur = joueur;
  }

  /* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
     RENDER ALL UI
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  function renderAll(){
    applyUIToPreset();
    if(!currentPreset){
      $('cw-svg-wrap').innerHTML = '<p class="cw-placeholder">Sélectionnez un modèle pour afficher le plan.</p>';
      $('cw-rh-tables').innerHTML = '';
      $('cw-lh-tables').innerHTML = '';
      $('cw-rows-cfg').innerHTML = '';
      return;
    }
    currentData = toData(currentPreset);
    currentData.nomJoueur = $('cw-nom-joueur').value.trim();
    var nomI = $('cw-nom-instrument').value.trim();
    if(nomI) currentData.nomInstrument = nomI;

    // SVG preview
    try {
      $('cw-svg-wrap').innerHTML = buildSVG_Plan(currentData, darkMode);
      bindSVGEditing();
    } catch(e){
      $('cw-svg-wrap').innerHTML = '<p style="color:#c0392b;padding:12px;">Erreur de rendu : '+e.message+'</p>';
    }

    renderRowsCfg();
    renderRHTables();
    renderLHTables();
  }

  /* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
     ROW CONFIGURATION TABLE
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  function refreshSVG(){
    if(!currentPreset)return;
    currentData=toData(currentPreset);
    currentData.nomJoueur=$('cw-nom-joueur').value.trim();
    var nomI=$('cw-nom-instrument').value.trim();if(nomI)currentData.nomInstrument=nomI;
    try{$('cw-svg-wrap').innerHTML=buildSVG_Plan(currentData,darkMode);bindSVGEditing();}catch(e){}
  }

  function renderRowsCfg(){
    if(!currentPreset) return;
    var rows = currentPreset.rangees || [];
    var html = '<table class="cw-cfg-table"><thead><tr><th>#</th><th>Nom</th><th>Boutons</th><th>Décalage</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
    rows.forEach(function(row, ri){
      html += '<tr>';
      html += '<td>'+(ri+1)+'</td>';
      html += '<td><input type="text" value="'+escAttr(row.nom||'')+'" data-row="'+ri+'" data-field="nom" class="cw-row-cfg-input"></td>';
      html += '<td><input type="number" min="1" max="30" value="'+(row.nb||0)+'" data-row="'+ri+'" data-field="nb" class="cw-row-cfg-input" style="width:60px"></td>';
      var off=row.offset||0;
      html += '<td><div class="cw-off-wrap">'
        +'<button type="button" class="cw-off-btn" data-row="'+ri+'" data-od="-1">−</button>'
        +'<input type="number" class="cw-input cw-off-input cw-row-cfg-input" min="-30" max="30" value="'+off+'" data-row="'+ri+'" data-field="offset">'
        +'<button type="button" class="cw-off-btn" data-row="'+ri+'" data-od="1">＋</button>'
        +'</div></td>';
      html += '</tr>';
    });
    html += '</tbody></table>';
    $('cw-rows-cfg').innerHTML = html;

    // Bind change events
    $('cw-rows-cfg').querySelectorAll('.cw-row-cfg-input').forEach(function(inp){
      inp.addEventListener('change', onRowCfgChange);
    });
    $('cw-rows-cfg').querySelectorAll('.cw-off-btn[data-od]').forEach(function(btn){
      btn.addEventListener('click',function(){
        var ri=parseInt(btn.getAttribute('data-row')),d=parseInt(btn.getAttribute('data-od'));
        if(!currentPreset||!currentPreset.rangees[ri])return;
        currentPreset.rangees[ri].offset=Math.max(-30,Math.min(30,(currentPreset.rangees[ri].offset||0)+d));
        renderRowsCfg();refreshSVG();
      });
    });
  }

  function onRowCfgChange(e){
    var inp = e.target;
    var ri = parseInt(inp.getAttribute('data-row'));
    var field = inp.getAttribute('data-field');
    if(!currentPreset || !currentPreset.rangees[ri]) return;
    if(field === 'nom'){
      currentPreset.rangees[ri].nom = inp.value;
    } else if(field === 'nb'){
      var newNb = Math.max(1, parseInt(inp.value)||1);
      var oldNb = currentPreset.rangees[ri].nb;
      currentPreset.rangees[ri].nb = newNb;
      // Adjust notes array
      var notes = currentPreset.notes.droite[ri] || [];
      if(newNb > oldNb){
        for(var k = oldNb; k < newNb; k++) notes.push({p:'',t:''});
      } else {
        notes.length = newNb;
      }
      currentPreset.notes.droite[ri]=notes;
    } else if(field==='offset'){
      currentPreset.rangees[ri].offset=Math.max(-30,Math.min(30,parseInt(inp.value)||0));
    }
    renderAll();
  }

  /* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
     RH NOTE EDITING TABLES
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  function renderRHTables(){
    if(!currentPreset) return;
    var notes = currentPreset.notes || {};
    var droite = notes.droite || [];
    var html = '';
    (currentPreset.rangees || []).forEach(function(row, ri){
      var btns = droite[ri] || [];
      html += '<table class="cw-note-table"><caption>'+escHTML(row.nom || ('Rangée '+(ri+1)))+'</caption>';
      html += '<thead><tr><th>#</th><th>\u2193 Poussé</th><th>\u2191 Tiré</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
      for(var bi = 0; bi < (row.nb||btns.length); bi++){
        var btn = btns[bi] || {p:'',t:''};
        html += '<tr>';
        html += '<td class="cw-num">'+(bi+1)+'</td>';
        html += '<td><input type="text" value="'+escAttr(btn.p||'')+'" data-section="rh" data-row="'+ri+'" data-btn="'+bi+'" data-dir="p" onfocus="cwShowPicker(this)" autocomplete="off"></td>';
        html += '<td><input type="text" value="'+escAttr(btn.t||'')+'" data-section="rh" data-row="'+ri+'" data-btn="'+bi+'" data-dir="t" onfocus="cwShowPicker(this)" autocomplete="off"></td>';
        html += '</tr>';
      }
      html += '</tbody></table>';
    });
    $('cw-rh-tables').innerHTML = html;
    $('cw-rh-tables').querySelectorAll('input[data-section="rh"]').forEach(function(inp){
      inp.addEventListener('change', onNoteChange);
    });
  }

  /* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
     LH NOTE EDITING TABLES
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  function renderLHTables(){
    if(!currentPreset) return;
    var notes = currentPreset.notes || {};
    var html = '';

    // Basses
    var basses = notes.basses || [];
    html += '<table class="cw-note-table"><caption>Basses</caption>';
    html += '<thead><tr><th>#</th><th>\u2193 Poussé</th><th>\u2191 Tiré</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
    for(var i = 0; i < basses.length; i++){
      var b = basses[i] || {p:'',t:''};
      html += '<tr>';
      html += '<td class="cw-num">'+(i+1)+'</td>';
      html += '<td><input type="text" value="'+escAttr(b.p||'')+'" data-section="basses" data-btn="'+i+'" data-dir="p" onfocus="cwShowPicker(this)" autocomplete="off"></td>';
      html += '<td><input type="text" value="'+escAttr(b.t||'')+'" data-section="basses" data-btn="'+i+'" data-dir="t" onfocus="cwShowPicker(this)" autocomplete="off"></td>';
      html += '</tr>';
    }
    html += '</tbody></table>';

    // Accords
    var accords = notes.accords || [];
    html += '<table class="cw-note-table"><caption>Accords</caption>';
    html += '<thead><tr><th>#</th><th>\u2193 Poussé</th><th>\u2191 Tiré</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
    for(var j = 0; j < accords.length; j++){
      var a = accords[j] || {p:'',t:''};
      html += '<tr>';
      html += '<td class="cw-num">'+(j+1)+'</td>';
      html += '<td><input type="text" value="'+escAttr(a.p||'')+'" data-section="accords" data-btn="'+j+'" data-dir="p" onfocus="cwShowPicker(this)" autocomplete="off"></td>';
      html += '<td><input type="text" value="'+escAttr(a.t||'')+'" data-section="accords" data-btn="'+j+'" data-dir="t" onfocus="cwShowPicker(this)" autocomplete="off"></td>';
      html += '</tr>';
    }
    html += '</tbody></table>';

    $('cw-lh-tables').innerHTML = html;
    $('cw-lh-tables').querySelectorAll('input[data-section]').forEach(function(inp){
      inp.addEventListener('change', onNoteChange);
    });
    if(!currentPreset.lhRows) currentPreset.lhRows=[{nb:(currentPreset.notes.basses||[]).length||6,offset:0}];
    var _lhR=currentPreset.lhRows;
    var lhCfg='<table class="cw-cfg-table" style="margin-top:10px"><caption style="font-size:.78rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--text2);text-align:left;padding-bottom:4px">Rangées main gauche</caption><thead><tr><th>#</th><th>Boutons</th><th>Décalage</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
    _lhR.forEach(function(row,ri){
      var off=row.offset||0;
      lhCfg+='<tr><td>'+(ri+1)+'</td>'
        +'<td><input type="number" min="1" max="30" value="'+(row.nb||6)+'" data-lhrow="'+ri+'" data-lhf="nb" class="cw-input cw-lhri" style="width:60px"></td>'
        +'<td><div class="cw-off-wrap">'
        +'<button type="button" class="cw-off-btn" data-lhrow="'+ri+'" data-lhd="-1">−</button>'
        +'<input type="number" class="cw-input cw-off-input cw-lhri" min="-30" max="30" value="'+off+'" data-lhrow="'+ri+'" data-lhf="offset">'
        +'<button type="button" class="cw-off-btn" data-lhrow="'+ri+'" data-lhd="1">＋</button>'
        +'</div></td></tr>';
    });
    lhCfg+='</tbody></table>';
    $('cw-lh-tables').insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend',lhCfg);
    $('cw-lh-tables').querySelectorAll('.cw-lhri').forEach(function(inp){
      inp.addEventListener('change',function(){
        var ri=parseInt(inp.getAttribute('data-lhrow')),f=inp.getAttribute('data-lhf');
        if(f==='nb') currentPreset.lhRows[ri].nb=Math.max(1,parseInt(inp.value)||1);
        if(f==='offset') currentPreset.lhRows[ri].offset=Math.max(-30,Math.min(30,parseInt(inp.value)||0));
        refreshSVG();
      });
    });
    $('cw-lh-tables').querySelectorAll('.cw-off-btn[data-lhd]').forEach(function(btn){
      btn.addEventListener('click',function(){
        var ri=parseInt(btn.getAttribute('data-lhrow')),d=parseInt(btn.getAttribute('data-lhd'));
        currentPreset.lhRows[ri].offset=Math.max(-30,Math.min(30,(currentPreset.lhRows[ri].offset||0)+d));
        renderLHTables();refreshSVG();
      });
    });
  }

  function onNoteChange(e){
    var inp = e.target;
    var section = inp.getAttribute('data-section');
    var bi = parseInt(inp.getAttribute('data-btn'));
    var dir = inp.getAttribute('data-dir');
    var val = inp.value.trim();
    if(!currentPreset) return;
    var notes = currentPreset.notes;
    if(section === 'rh'){
      var ri = parseInt(inp.getAttribute('data-row'));
      if(!notes.droite[ri]) notes.droite[ri] = [];
      if(!notes.droite[ri][bi]) notes.droite[ri][bi] = {p:'',t:''};
      notes.droite[ri][bi][dir] = val;
    } else if(section === 'basses'){
      if(!notes.basses[bi]) notes.basses[bi] = {p:'',t:''};
      notes.basses[bi][dir] = val;
    } else if(section === 'accords'){
      if(!notes.accords[bi]) notes.accords[bi] = {p:'',t:''};
      notes.accords[bi][dir] = val;
    }
    // Re-render SVG only (not the tables, to keep focus)
    applyUIToPreset();
    currentData = toData(currentPreset);
    currentData.nomJoueur = $('cw-nom-joueur').value.trim();
    var nomI = $('cw-nom-instrument').value.trim();
    if(nomI) currentData.nomInstrument = nomI;
    try {
      $('cw-svg-wrap').innerHTML = buildSVG_Plan(currentData, darkMode);
      bindSVGEditing();
    } catch(err){
      $('cw-svg-wrap').innerHTML = '<p style="color:#c0392b;padding:12px;">Erreur de rendu : '+err.message+'</p>';
    }
  }

  /* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
     HELPERS
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  function escAttr(s){
    return String(s||'').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;');
  }
  function escHTML(s){
    if(!s) return '';
    var d = document.createElement('div');
    d.appendChild(document.createTextNode(String(s)));
    return d.innerHTML;
  }

  function showToast(msg, duration){
    var el = $('cw-toast');
    el.textContent = msg;
    el.style.display = 'block';
    clearTimeout(el._timer);
    el._timer = setTimeout(function(){ el.style.display = 'none'; }, duration || 2500);
  }

  /* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
     EXPORT JSON (clipboard)
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

  /* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
     SNAPSHOT — format compatible outil offline
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  function cwSnapshotPreset(){
    if(!currentPreset) return null;
    applyUIToPreset();
    var nom = $('cw-nom-instrument').value.trim() || 'Sans titre';
    var joueur = $('cw-nom-joueur').value.trim();
    return {
      id: currentPreset.id || Date.now().toString(),
      nom: nom,
      joueur: joueur,
      luthier: currentPreset.luthier || "Ewen d'Aviau",
      dateCreation: currentPreset.dateCreation || new Date().toISOString().substring(0,10),
      lastModified: new Date().toISOString(),
      nbRangees: (currentPreset.rangees||[]).length,
      rangees: JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(currentPreset.rangees||[])),
      nbVoix: currentPreset.nbVoix || 2,
      voixPerRow: currentPreset.voixPerRow || [],
      nbVoixAccords: currentPreset.nbVoixAccords || 2,
      nbVoixBasses: currentPreset.nbVoixBasses || 2,
      lhDisplayMode: currentPreset.lhDisplayMode || 'separated',
      lhPairedDir: currentPreset.lhPairedDir || 'vertical',
      lhRows: JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(currentPreset.lhRows || [{nb:(currentPreset.notes&&currentPreset.notes.basses?currentPreset.notes.basses.length:6),offset:0}])),
      lhPairsPerRow: currentPreset.lhPairsPerRow || 2,
      lhBassFirst: currentPreset.lhBassFirst || false,
      notes: JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(currentPreset.notes||{}))
    };
  }

  function buildExportText(){
    if(!currentPreset) return '';
    applyUIToPreset();
    var pr=currentPreset;
    var nom=($('cw-nom-instrument').value.trim()||pr.nom||pr.label||'Sans titre');
    var joueur=$('cw-nom-joueur').value.trim();
    var date=new Date().toLocaleDateString('fr-FR');
    var pad=function(s,n){s=String(s);while(s.length<n)s=' '+s;return s;};
    var lines=['══════════════════════════════════','  '+nom];
    if(joueur)lines.push('  Joueur : '+joueur);
    lines.push('  '+date,'══════════════════════════════════','','MAIN DROITE','──────────────────────────────────');
    (pr.rangees||[]).forEach(function(row,ri){
      var label=row.nom||('Rangée '+(ri+1));
      if(row.offset) label+=' (décalage '+(row.offset>0?'+':'')+row.offset+')';
      lines.push('  '+label);
      var btns=((pr.notes||{}).droite||[])[ri]||[];
      for(var bi=0;bi<(row.nb||btns.length);bi++){
        var b=btns[bi]||{p:'',t:''};
        lines.push('    '+pad(bi+1,2)+'.  ↓ '+pad(b.p||'–',8)+'  ↑ '+(b.t||'–'));
      }
    });
    var basses=(pr.notes||{}).basses||[];
    var accords=(pr.notes||{}).accords||[];
    if(basses.length||accords.length){
      lines.push('','MAIN GAUCHE','──────────────────────────────────');
      if(basses.length){
        var lhOff=(pr.lhRows&#038;&#038;pr.lhRows[0]&#038;&#038;pr.lhRows[0].offset)?(' (décalage '+(pr.lhRows[0].offset>0?'+':'')+pr.lhRows[0].offset+')'):'';
        lines.push('  Basses'+lhOff);
        basses.forEach(function(b,i){lines.push('    '+pad(i+1,2)+'.  ↓ '+pad(b.p||'–',8)+'  ↑ '+(b.t||'–'));});
      }
      if(accords.length){
        lines.push('  Accords');
        accords.forEach(function(a,i){lines.push('    '+pad(i+1,2)+'.  ↓ '+pad(a.p||'–',8)+'  ↑ '+(a.t||'–'));});
      }
    }
    lines.push('','══════════════════════════════════');
    return lines.join('\n');
  }

  function exportText(){
    var txt=buildExportText();
    if(!txt){showToast('Aucun plan à exporter.');return;}
    if(navigator.clipboard&&navigator.clipboard.writeText){
      navigator.clipboard.writeText(txt).then(function(){showToast('✔ Texte copié dans le presse-papiers');}).catch(function(){fallbackCopy(txt);});
    } else {fallbackCopy(txt);}
  }

  function fallbackCopy(text){
    var ta = document.createElement('textarea');
    ta.value = text;
    ta.style.position = 'fixed';
    ta.style.left = '-9999px';
    document.body.appendChild(ta);
    ta.select();
    try { document.execCommand('copy'); showToast('JSON copié \u2714'); }
    catch(e){ showToast('Impossible de copier. Copiez manuellement.'); }
    document.body.removeChild(ta);
  }

  /* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
     TEMPLATE MANAGEMENT (localStorage)
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  function getSavedPlans(){
    try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(LS_KEY)) || {}; }
    catch(e){ return {}; }
  }
  function setSavedPlans(plans){
    localStorage.setItem(LS_KEY, JSON.stringify(plans));
  }
  function refreshSavedList(){
    var sel = $('cw-saved-sel');
    sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">— Aucun plan sauvegardé —</option>';
    var plans = getSavedPlans();
    var keys = Object.keys(plans).sort();
    if(keys.length){
      sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">— Choisir un plan —</option>';
      keys.forEach(function(k){
        var opt = document.createElement('option');
        opt.value = k;
        opt.textContent = k;
        sel.appendChild(opt);
      });
    }
  }
  function savePlan(){
    var snap = cwSnapshotPreset();
    if(!snap){ showToast('Aucun plan à sauvegarder.'); return; }
    var suggested = prompt('Nom du plan :', snap.nom);
    if(!suggested) return;
    snap.nom = suggested;
    currentPreset.id = snap.id;
    var plans = getSavedPlans();
    plans[suggested] = snap;
    setSavedPlans(plans);
    refreshSavedList();
    showToast('Plan « '+suggested+' » sauvegardé \u2714');
  }
  function loadPlan(){
    var key = $('cw-saved-sel').value;
    if(!key){ showToast('Sélectionnez un plan.'); return; }
    var plans = getSavedPlans();
    if(!plans[key]){ showToast('Plan introuvable.'); return; }
    currentPreset = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(plans[key]));
    // Update UI fields
    $('cw-nom-instrument').value = currentPreset.nom || currentPreset.label || '';
    $('cw-nom-joueur').value = currentPreset.joueur || '';
    $('cw-preset-sel').value = '';
    renderAll();
    showToast('Plan « '+key+' » chargé \u2714');
  }
  function deletePlan(){
    var key = $('cw-saved-sel').value;
    if(!key){ showToast('Sélectionnez un plan.'); return; }
    if(!confirm('Supprimer « '+key+' » ?')) return;
    var plans = getSavedPlans();
    delete plans[key];
    setSavedPlans(plans);
    refreshSavedList();
    showToast('Plan supprimé.');
  }

  function cwNormalisePreset(json){
    if(Array.isArray(json)) json = json[0];
    return json || null;
  }

  function loadFromFile(event){
    var file = event.target.files[0];
    if(!file) return;
    var reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = function(e){
      try {
        var json = JSON.parse(e.target.result);
        json = cwNormalisePreset(json);
        if(!json){ showToast('Format non reconnu'); return; }
        currentPreset = json;
        $('cw-nom-instrument').value = json.nom || '';
        $('cw-nom-joueur').value = json.joueur || '';
        renderAll();
        showToast('\u2714 Fichier chargé (format compatible outil offline)');
      } catch(ex){ showToast('Erreur: JSON invalide'); }
    };
    reader.readAsText(file);
  }

  /* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
     DARK/LIGHT TOGGLE
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  function toggleTheme(){
    darkMode = !darkMode;
    widget.classList.toggle('cw-dark', darkMode);
    $('cw-theme-toggle').textContent = darkMode ? '☀️' : '🌙';
    if(currentPreset) renderAll();
  }

  /* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
     COLLAPSIBLE SECTIONS
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  function initCollapsible(){
    widget.querySelectorAll('.cw-section-head[data-toggle]').forEach(function(head){
      head.addEventListener('click', function(){
        var targetId = head.getAttribute('data-toggle');
        var body = $(targetId);
        if(!body) return;
        var hidden = body.classList.contains('cw-hidden');
        body.classList.toggle('cw-hidden', !hidden);
        head.textContent = head.textContent.replace(/^[▶▼]/, hidden ? '▼' : '▶');
      });
    });
  }


  /* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
     SVG CLICK-TO-EDIT (popup édition poussé / tiré)
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  var _editCurrent = null;

  function bindSVGEditing(){
    if(!widget) return;
    widget.querySelectorAll('.cw-edit-btn').forEach(function(g){
      g.addEventListener('click', function(e){
        e.stopPropagation();
        openEditPopup(g.getAttribute('data-edit'), e);
      });
    });
  }

  function openEditPopup(editId, e){
    if(!currentPreset || !editId) return;
    var parts = editId.split(':');
    var btn = null, title = '';
    if(parts[0] === 'rh'){
      var ri = parseInt(parts[1]), bi = parseInt(parts[2]);
      var row = (currentPreset.rangees || [])[ri];
      var rowNotes = ((currentPreset.notes || {}).droite || [])[ri] || [];
      btn = rowNotes[bi] || {p:'', t:''};
      title = (row ? row.nom : 'Rangée '+(ri+1)) + ' — Bouton '+(bi+1);
      _editCurrent = {src:'rh', ri:ri, bi:bi};
    } else {
      var src = parts[0];
      var idx = parseInt(parts[1]);
      var arr = ((currentPreset.notes || {})[src] || []);
      btn = arr[idx] || {p:'', t:''};
      var srcLabel = src === 'basses' ? 'Basse' : src === 'accords' ? 'Accord' : 'Terzetto';
      title = srcLabel + ' '+(idx+1);
      _editCurrent = {src:src, idx:idx};
    }
    $('cw-ep-title').textContent = title;
    $('cw-ep-push').value = btn.p || '';
    $('cw-ep-pull').value = btn.t || '';
    var popup = $('cw-edit-popup');
    popup.classList.remove('cw-hidden');
    var pw = popup.offsetWidth || 220, ph = popup.offsetHeight || 160;
    var left = Math.min(e.clientX + 8, window.innerWidth  - pw - 8);
    var top  = Math.min(e.clientY + 8, window.innerHeight - ph - 8);
    popup.style.left = Math.max(8, left) + 'px';
    popup.style.top  = Math.max(8, top)  + 'px';
    $('cw-ep-push').focus();
    $('cw-ep-push').select();
  }

  function closeEditPopup(){
    $('cw-edit-popup').classList.add('cw-hidden');
    _editCurrent = null;
  }

  function saveEditPopup(){
    if(!_editCurrent || !currentPreset) return;
    var p = $('cw-ep-push').value.trim();
    var t = $('cw-ep-pull').value.trim();
    var notes = currentPreset.notes || (currentPreset.notes = {});
    if(_editCurrent.src === 'rh'){
      var ri = _editCurrent.ri, bi = _editCurrent.bi;
      if(!notes.droite)       notes.droite       = [];
      if(!notes.droite[ri])   notes.droite[ri]   = [];
      if(!notes.droite[ri][bi]) notes.droite[ri][bi] = {};
      notes.droite[ri][bi].p = p;
      notes.droite[ri][bi].t = t;
    } else {
      var src2 = _editCurrent.src, idx2 = _editCurrent.idx;
      if(!notes[src2])        notes[src2]        = [];
      if(!notes[src2][idx2])  notes[src2][idx2]  = {};
      notes[src2][idx2].p = p;
      notes[src2][idx2].t = t;
    }
    closeEditPopup();
    currentData = toData(currentPreset);
    currentData.nomJoueur = $('cw-nom-joueur').value.trim();
    var nomI = $('cw-nom-instrument').value.trim();
    if(nomI) currentData.nomInstrument = nomI;
    try {
      $('cw-svg-wrap').innerHTML = buildSVG_Plan(currentData, darkMode);
      bindSVGEditing();
    } catch(e2){ /* ignore */ }
  }

  /* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
     INIT
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  function init(){
    populatePresetSelector();
    initCollapsible();
    refreshSavedList();

    // Event listeners
    $('cw-preset-sel').addEventListener('change', function(){
      loadPreset(this.value);
    });
    $('cw-nom-instrument').addEventListener('input', function(){
      if(currentPreset) renderAll();
    });
    $('cw-nom-joueur').addEventListener('input', function(){
      if(currentPreset) renderAll();
    });
    $('cw-theme-toggle').addEventListener('click', toggleTheme);
    $('cw-export-btn').addEventListener('click', exportText);
    $('cw-save-btn').addEventListener('click', savePlan);
    $('cw-load-btn').addEventListener('click', loadPlan);
    $('cw-delete-btn').addEventListener('click', deletePlan);

    // Edit popup events
    $('cw-ep-save').addEventListener('click', saveEditPopup);
    $('cw-ep-cancel').addEventListener('click', closeEditPopup);
    [$('cw-ep-push'), $('cw-ep-pull')].forEach(function(inp){
      inp.addEventListener('keydown', function(ev){
        if(ev.key === 'Enter')  saveEditPopup();
        if(ev.key === 'Escape') closeEditPopup();
      });
    });
    document.addEventListener('click', function(ev){
      var popup = $('cw-edit-popup');
      if(popup && !popup.classList.contains('cw-hidden') && !popup.contains(ev.target)){
        closeEditPopup();
      }
      var picker = $('cw-note-picker');
      if(picker && !picker.classList.contains('cw-hidden') && !picker.contains(ev.target)
         && ev.target.getAttribute && !ev.target.getAttribute('onfocus')){
        cwHidePicker();
      }
    });
    initCwPicker();
  }

  // Run init when DOM is ready
  if(document.readyState === 'loading'){
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init);
  } else {
    init();
  }

})();
</script>
        </div>
            </div>
</div>

            </div> <!-- .nm-page-wrap -->

								if ( !( captcha_div.offsetWidth || captcha_div.offsetHeight || captcha_div.getClientRects().length ) ) {					    	
									if ( jetpack_sso == null && ! form.classList.contains( 'woocommerce-form-login' ) ) {
										continue;
									}
								}
							}

							let alreadyCloned = form.querySelector( '.c4wp-submit' );
							if ( null != alreadyCloned ) {
								continue;
							}

							let foundSubmitBtn = form.querySelector( '#signup-form [type=submit], [type=submit]:not(#group-creation-create):not([name="signup_submit"]):not([name="ac_form_submit"]):not(.verify-captcha)' );
							let cloned = false;
							let clone  = false;

							// Submit button found, clone it.
							if ( foundSubmitBtn ) {
								clone = foundSubmitBtn.cloneNode(true);
								clone.classList.add( 'c4wp-submit' );
								clone.removeAttribute( 'onclick' );
								clone.removeAttribute( 'onkeypress' );
								if ( foundSubmitBtn.parentElement.form === null ) {
									foundSubmitBtn.parentElement.prepend(clone);
								} else {
									foundSubmitBtn.parentElement.insertBefore( clone, foundSubmitBtn );
								}
								foundSubmitBtn.style.display = "none";
								captcha_div                  = form.querySelector( '.c4wp_captcha_field_div' );
								cloned = true;
							}

							// WC block checkout clone btn.
							if ( has_wc_submit && ! form.classList.contains( 'c4wp-primed' ) ) {
								clone = wcblock_submit.cloneNode(true);
								clone.classList.add( 'c4wp-submit' );
								clone.classList.add( 'c4wp-clone' );
								clone.removeAttribute( 'onclick' );
								clone.removeAttribute( 'onkeypress' );
								if ( wcblock_submit.parentElement.form === null ) {
									wcblock_submit.parentElement.prepend(clone);
								} else {
									wcblock_submit.parentElement.insertBefore( clone, wcblock_submit );
								}
								wcblock_submit.style.display = "none";

								clone.addEventListener('click', function( e ){
									if ( form.classList.contains( 'c4wp_v2_fallback_active' ) ) {
										jQuery( form ).find( '.wc-block-components-checkout-place-order-button:not(.c4wp-submit)' ).click(); 
										return true;
									} else {
										grecaptcha.execute( '6LfrNp8hAAAAANP3iy0WZbM7p_N8KjOK1IkOr-EL', ).then( function( data ) {
											form.classList.add( 'c4wp-primed' );
										});	
									}

								});
								foundSubmitBtn = wcblock_submit;
								cloned = true;
							}
							
							// Clone created, listen to its click.
							if ( cloned ) {
								clone.addEventListener( 'click', function ( event ) {
									logSubmit( event, 'cloned', form, foundSubmitBtn );
								});
							// No clone, execute and watch for form submission.
							} else {
								grecaptcha.execute(
									'6LfrNp8hAAAAANP3iy0WZbM7p_N8KjOK1IkOr-EL',
								).then( function( data ) {
									var responseElem = form.querySelector( '.c4wp_response' );
									if ( responseElem == null ) {
										var responseElem = document.querySelector( '.c4wp_response' );
									}
									if ( responseElem != null ) {
										responseElem.setAttribute( 'value', data );	
									}									
								});

								// Anything else.
								form.addEventListener( 'submit', function ( event ) {
									logSubmit( event, 'other', form );
								});	
							}

							function logSubmit( event, form_type = '', form, foundSubmitBtn ) {
								// Standard v3 check.
								if ( ! form.classList.contains( 'c4wp_v2_fallback_active' ) && ! form.classList.contains( 'c4wp_verified' ) ) {
									event.preventDefault();
									try {
										grecaptcha.execute(
											'6LfrNp8hAAAAANP3iy0WZbM7p_N8KjOK1IkOr-EL',
										).then( function( data ) {	
											var responseElem = form.querySelector( '.c4wp_response' );
											if ( responseElem == null ) {
												var responseElem = document.querySelector( '.c4wp_response' );
											}
											
											responseElem.setAttribute( 'value', data );	

											if ( form.classList.contains( 'wc-block-checkout__form' ) ) {
												// WC block checkout.
												let input = document.querySelector('input[id*="c4wp-wc-checkout"]'); 
												let lastValue = input.value;
												var token = data;
												input.value = token;
												let event = new Event('input', { bubbles: true });
												event.simulated = true;
												let tracker = input._valueTracker;
												if (tracker) {
													tracker.setValue( lastValue );
												}
												input.dispatchEvent(event)												
											}

														
			/* @v3-fallback-js:start */
			if ( typeof captcha_div == 'undefined' && form.classList.contains( 'wc-block-checkout__form' ) ) {
				var captcha_div = form.querySelector( '#additional-information-c4wp-c4wp-wc-checkout' );
			}

			if ( ! captcha_div && form.classList.contains( 'wc-block-checkout__form' ) ) {
				var captcha_div = form.querySelector( '#order-c4wp-c4wp-wc-checkout' );
			}

			if ( typeof captcha_div == 'undefined' ) {
				var captcha_div = form.querySelector( '.c4wp_captcha_field_div' );
			}

			var parentElem = captcha_div.parentElement;

			if ( ( form.classList.contains( 'c4wp-primed' ) ) || ( ! form.classList.contains( 'c4wp_verify_underway' ) && captcha_div.parentElement.getAttribute( 'data-c4wp-use-ajax' ) == 'true' ) ) {

				form.classList.add('c4wp_verify_underway' );
				const flagMarkup =  '<input id="c4wp_ajax_flag" type="hidden" name="c4wp_ajax_flag" value="c4wp_ajax_flag">';
				var flagMarkupDiv = document.createElement('div');
				flagMarkupDiv.innerHTML = flagMarkup.trim();

				form.appendChild( flagMarkupDiv );
	
				var nonce = captcha_div.parentElement.getAttribute( 'data-nonce' );

				var formData = new FormData();

				formData.append( 'action', 'c4wp_ajax_verify' );
				formData.append( 'nonce', nonce );
				formData.append( 'response', data );
				
				fetch( 'https://ewendaviau.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php', {
					method: 'POST',
					body: formData,
				} ) // wrapped
					.then( 
						res => res.json()
					)
					.then( data => {
						if ( data['success'] ) {
							form.classList.add( 'c4wp_verified' );
							// Submit as usual.
							if ( foundSubmitBtn ) {
								foundSubmitBtn.click();
							} else if ( form.classList.contains( 'wc-block-checkout__form' ) ) {
								jQuery( form ).find( '.wc-block-components-checkout-place-order-button:not(.c4wp-submit)' ).click(); 
							} else {								
								if ( typeof form.submit === 'function' ) {
									form.submit();
								} else {
									HTMLFormElement.prototype.submit.call(form);
								}
							}

						} else {
							//jQuery( '.nf-form-cont' ).trigger( 'nfFormReady' );

							if ( 'redirect' === 'v2_checkbox' ) {
								window.location.href = '';
							}

							if ( 'v2_checkbox' === 'v2_checkbox' ) {
								if ( form.classList.contains( 'wc-block-checkout__form' ) ) {
									captcha_div = captcha_div.parentElement;
								}

								captcha_div.innerHTML = '';
								form.classList.add( 'c4wp_v2_fallback_active' );
								flagMarkupDiv.firstChild.setAttribute( 'name', 'c4wp_v2_fallback' );

								var c4wp_captcha = grecaptcha.render( captcha_div,{
									'sitekey' : '6Lcq73sqAAAAAGbVV2-NlwpqI6Grlt0nc2Yg5n8P',		
									'size'  : 'normal',
									'theme' : 'light',				
									'expired-callback' : function(){
										grecaptcha.reset( c4wp_captcha );
									}
								}); 
								jQuery( '.ninja-forms-field.c4wp-submit' ).prop( 'disabled', false );
							}

							if ( form.classList.contains( 'wc-block-checkout__form' ) ) {
								return true;
							}

							if ( form.parentElement.classList.contains( 'nf-form-layout' ) ) {
								jQuery( '.ninja-forms-field.c4wp-submit' ).prop( 'disabled', false );
								return false;
							}

							// Prevent further submission
							event.preventDefault();
							return false;
						}
					} )
					.catch( err => console.error( err ) );

				// Prevent further submission
				event.preventDefault();
				return false;
			}
			/* @v3-fallback-js:end */
			
			
											// Submit as usual.
											if ( foundSubmitBtn ) {
												foundSubmitBtn.click();
											} else if ( form.classList.contains( 'wc-block-checkout__form' ) ) {
												jQuery( form ).find( '.wc-block-components-checkout-place-order-button:not(.c4wp-submit)' ).click(); 
											} else {
												
												if ( typeof form.submit === 'function' ) {
													form.submit();
												} else {
													HTMLFormElement.prototype.submit.call(form);
												}
											}

											return true;
										});
									} catch (e) {
										// Silence.
									}
								// V2 fallback.
								} else {
									if ( form.classList.contains( 'wpforms-form' ) || form.classList.contains( 'frm-fluent-form' ) || form.classList.contains( 'woocommerce-checkout' ) ) {
										return true;
									}

									if ( form.parentElement.classList.contains( 'nf-form-layout' ) ) {
										return false;
									}
									
									if ( form.classList.contains( 'wc-block-checkout__form' ) ) {
										return;
									}
									
									// Submit as usual.
									if ( typeof form.submit === 'function' ) {
										form.submit();
									} else {
										HTMLFormElement.prototype.submit.call(form);
									}

									return true;
								}
							};
						}
					};

					grecaptcha.ready( c4wp_onloadCallback );

					if ( typeof jQuery !== 'undefined' ) {
						jQuery( 'body' ).on( 'click', '.acomment-reply.bp-primary-action', function ( e ) {
							c4wp_onloadCallback();
						});	
					}

					//token is valid for 2 minutes, So get new token every after 1 minutes 50 seconds
					setInterval(c4wp_onloadCallback, 110000);

					
					window.addEventListener("load", (event) => {
						if ( typeof jQuery !== 'undefined' && jQuery( 'input[id*="c4wp-wc-checkout"]' ).length ) {
							var element = document.createElement('div');
							var html = '<div class="c4wp_captcha_field" style="margin-bottom: 10px" data-nonce="710f077c51" data-c4wp-use-ajax="true" data-c4wp-v2-site-key="6Lcq73sqAAAAAGbVV2-NlwpqI6Grlt0nc2Yg5n8P"><div id="c4wp_captcha_field_0" class="c4wp_captcha_field_div"><input type="hidden" name="g-recaptcha-response" class="c4wp_response" aria-label="do not use" aria-readonly="true" value="" /></div></div>';
							element.innerHTML = html;
							jQuery( '[class*="c4wp-wc-checkout"]' ).append( element );
							jQuery( '[class*="c4wp-wc-checkout"]' ).find('*').off();
							c4wp_onloadCallback();
						}
					});
				/* @v3-js:end */
			</script>
			<!-- / CAPTCHA by CAPTCHA 4WP plugin -->        
        </div> <!-- .nm-page-overflow -->
	</body>
</html>
